          result = matrix(nrow=length(arr[[1]]), ncol = 675)
          for(i in 1:length(arr[[1]]))
          {
            temp <- strsplit(arr[[1]][i], ",")

            {
              if(temp[[1]][j] == "1")
              {
                result[i,j]=1
              }
              if(temp[[1]][j] == "0")
              {
                result[i,j]=0
              }

              {
                result[i,j]=NA
              }
            }
          }
